# Skill 6 Blended-Persona Kanban v2 — MASTER VERIFICATION LEDGER (117-unit, PENDING)

> Source of truth: MASTER SPEC v2 Section E.2. One row per unit, U1-U117. Fresh 117-unit pending ledger (supersedes the stale 105-unit version).
> Status legend: `pending` -> (in-progress) -> `merged` -> `verified`. No unit is `done` until BOTH merged AND judge-verified at the standing 8.5 gate.
> The `[<Model> x<count>]` label column is the per-unit model/agent assignment, filled at dispatch. Blank = not yet assigned.

> **OPERATOR DECISION 2026-07-14 — Anthology GHL authentication (U69/U70/U71) — RESOLVED/BINDING:** the Anthology↔GHL authentication gating **U69** (GK-07, publish the 3 draft Anthology release-notification workflows + re-cut the snapshot), **U70** (GK-08, provision `chapter_rewrite1`/`chapter_rewrite2` custom fields), and **U71** (GK-09, clear the WAF/edge 403 on `verify-imported` + run the snapshot chain) is **PER-CLIENT, CLIENT-OWNED tokens**. Each client provides their own GoHighLevel Private Integration Token (PIT); the Anthology engine authenticates with that client's own token. There is NO shared operator token, no cross-client comingling — aligned with the standing sovereignty rule (clients own their credentials, operator never substitutes). Resolved by the operator Trevor, 2026-07-14; binding on U69/U70/U71's build agents, not an open question. Full ruling recorded in MASTER SPEC v2 Section E.3 ("OPERATOR DECISION 2026-07-14 — Anthology GHL authentication"). No unit status below changed by this note — U69/U70/U71 remain `pending` until actually built.

> 🔒 **OPERATOR RULINGS 2026-07-14 — D2, D3, D5 RATIFIED — BINDING SPEC. Do not reinterpret or re-litigate.**
>
> **D2 (D-A2) — RATIFIED: ROLE COUNT.** A COLLAPSED blend **SATISFIES** the min-2 invariant by ROLE count (voice-role + topic-role), even when a single persona id fills both. The receipt MUST record `collapsed=true` (plus the reason) so every collapse is auditable. Below-min drift on CONFIRMED bundles still alerts via the board-hygiene companion. This honors BOTH the operator-confirmed 2026-07-08 collapse design AND the min-2 invariant literally — neither silently deprecates the other.
>   → `validate_blend_invariant(bundle) -> {ok, count, roles, reason}` counts **ROLES**, not distinct persona ids.
>   → Migration 090 already carries the `voice_collapsed` mirror column — `collapsed=true` has a home TODAY. **No new migration needed.**
>   → The validator RECORDS and ALERTS; it must **never BLOCK** a write path. That is what makes this reversible.
>
> **D3 (D-A3) — RATIFIED:** the allowlist at `v2-autonomous-build-sop.md:292-293` governs the **TASK/CONVERSION SLOT ONLY**. VOICE and SUBSTANCE come from the blend.
>
> **D5 (B-D1) — RATIFIED: KILL the 5-surname copy cap.** VOICE = any of the 99 catalog personas. The copy-craft TASK slot must come from `copy_craft_pool` (the five plus `edwards-*` plus the Brunson-family crosswalk targets), defined ONCE in `shared-utils/persona-crosswalk.json`, referenced by BOTH Standard Operating Procedures, machine-validated by `persona_crosswalk.py --validate`.
>
> Ratified by the operator Trevor, 2026-07-14; binding on U6/U7/U18's build agents, not an open question. Full ruling recorded VERBATIM in MASTER SPEC v2 Section E.3 ("OPERATOR RULINGS 2026-07-14 — D2, D3, D5 RATIFIED"). **U6 (D2), U18 (D5), and U7 (D3) are no longer decision-blocked** — the DECISION gate is resolved; this does NOT change any unit's build status below. U6, U7, and U18 remain `pending` until actually built. No other decision item (D4, D6–D23) is affected by this note.

> 🐛 **DEFECT FIX 2026-07-15 — ARCHIVAL RAIL (Option A GitHub archival, D6/B-D2), FOUND BY U22 LIVE PROOF, REPRODUCED BY TWO INDEPENDENT OPUS INSTANCES:** in `06-ghl-install-pages/tools/ghl_github_archive.py`, `_http_request(method, url, body, *, token)` declares `token` KEYWORD-ONLY, but its 5 real-path callers (`resolve_authenticated_owner` ~277, `ensure_repo` ~296/~305-309, `put_file` ~325/~339) all passed it POSITIONALLY. On the LIVE path (`requester=None`) every GitHub API call raised `TypeError: _http_request() takes 3 positional arguments but 4 were given` before the token was ever used — no repo was ever created (fails on the first `GET /user`), so the archival rail NEVER archived on the live path despite the offline U24 mock-only suite staying green (its injected `requester` fixtures accept 4 plain positional args, masking the defect). Sibling `06-ghl-install-pages/tools/ghl_vercel.py` was already correct (`token=token` at its 3 call sites ~389/419/485) — used as the fix template. **FIX:** changed all 5 real callers in `ghl_github_archive.py` to `token=token`, matching `ghl_vercel.py`'s convention; kept the defensive keyword-only signature as-is. **NEW REGRESSION TEST** (`TestLivePathTokenKwarg` in `tests/test_ghl_github_archive.py`): exercises the LIVE path (`requester=None`) end-to-end — `test_resolve_authenticated_owner_live_path` (direct, unwrapped repro) and `test_run_archive_task_live_path_end_to_end` (full pipeline, all 5 call sites) — stubbing ONLY `urllib.request.urlopen` (the lowest-level transport), never the `_http_request`/`requester` seam, so this whole class of defect is now caught offline going forward. Proven to FAIL on the unfixed tree (captured pre-fix: both tests fail — the direct test raises `TypeError: _http_request() takes 3 positional arguments but 4 were given` uncaught; the pipeline test's receipt comes back `action=failed` with `error` = that same TypeError text) and PASS after the fix (32/32 in `test_ghl_github_archive.py`; 91/91 across `test_ghl_github_archive.py` + `test_ghl_github_reconcile.py` + `test_ghl_archive_receipt_gate.py` + `test_ghl_vercel.py`; module `--selftest` PASS). Full repo suite run for regression-scope check: 1615 passed, 15 skipped, 3 pre-existing failures confirmed unrelated (identical on a clean unmodified `origin/main` checkout, before this branch's changes: `test_ghl_iframe_drag.py::test_live_selftest_places_tile_across_cross_origin_iframe`, `test_ghl_secret_hygiene.py::TestRepoSourceHygiene::test_no_client_identifiers_in_new_files` [flags this ledger file's own U22 prose, pre-existing content, untouched by this fix], `test_survey_builder_hardening.py::test_skill_version_lockstep` [expects `v19.x`, repo is at `v20.0.35`, pre-existing version drift]). Built in a fresh dedicated worktree off latest `origin/main` (`c8e87fd1`, fetched fresh — NOT the dirty `~/openclaw-onboarding` clone or any `~/wt/*` worktree). Branch `fix/archival-rail-token-kwarg-20260715-053412` (tip `524bbdae`), QC 9.3 pass.
>
